Of the 81 cells there are 10 mismatches between the two footprints. The footprint-based conformance therefore is <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-110-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-376" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 126px; height: 0px; font-size: 132%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.158em, 1000em, 2.779em, -0.404em); top: -2.219em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-377" class="mrow"><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-378" class="mn">1</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-379" class="mo">−</span><span style="padding-left: 0.342em; padding-right: 0.12em;" id="MathJax-Span-380" class="mfrac"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.878em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.342em, -0.428em); top: -2.592em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.379em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-381" class="mn">10</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.342em, -0.457em); top: -1.782em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.379em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-382" class="mn">81</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.852em, 1000em, 1.245em, -0.487em); top: -1.302em; left: 0em;"><span style="border-left: 0.878em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 1.25px; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.082em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.278em;" id="MathJax-Span-383" class="mo">=</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.278em;" id="MathJax-Span-384" class="mn">0.8765</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.219em;"></span></span></span><span style="border-left: 0em solid; <br><br>
Footprint-based conformance is explained in detail in lecture 4.4: 'Conformance checking using causal footprints'.</div>

<h3 class="course-quiz-question-number">Question 5</h3>
<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-text">Given the process model below and the following event log: [ &lt; a,b,d&gt;<span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-111-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-385" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 15px; height: 0px; font-size: 132%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.168em, 1000em, 2.327em, -0.487em); top: -2.165em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-386" class="mrow"><span id="MathJax-Span-387" class="msubsup"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.833em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.842em, 1000em, 4.167em, -0.487em); top: -4.004em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-388" class="mi"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.004em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -2.527em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-389" class="texatom"><span id="MathJax-Span-390" class="mrow"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-391" class="mn">10</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="border-left: 0em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 1.244em; vertical-align: -0.071em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script id="MathJax-Element-111" type="math/tex">^{10}</script> ]

<br>
What is the correct token-based conformance?</div>

<td class="course-quiz-student-answer" dir="auto">
<input dir="auto" class="course-quiz-input" name="answer[1828dd2a7179820778d5ee8916ba54fc][]" id="gensym_548af5905d1eb" value="ddd7dab446ae2bc9cc6c8d5390acb391" disabled="" type="radio"><a href="https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/procmin/images/Quizzes/Quiz4-Q5%20variant%203.png" target="_blank"><img src="https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/procmin/images/Quizzes/Quiz4-Q5%20variant%203.png" width="500"></a>
<br>
Hence the token-based conformance is <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-112-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-392" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 270px; height: 0px; font-size: 132%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.116em, 1000em, 2.829em, -0.404em); top: -2.219em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-393" class="mrow"><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-394" class="mn">1</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-395" class="mo">−</span><span style="padding-left: 0.342em; padding-right: 0.12em;" id="MathJax-Span-396" class="mfrac"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 4.774em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.385em, -0.428em); top: -2.634em; left: 50%; margin-left: -1.028em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-397" class="mrow"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-571" class="mo">×</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-572" class="mn">0.80</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-573" class="mo">+</span><span style="padding-left: 0.342em; padding-right: 0.12em;" id="MathJax-Span-574" class="mfrac"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.499em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.327em, -0.428em); top: -2.576em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.189em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-575" class="mn">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.327em, -0.452em); top: -1.782em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.189em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-576" class="mn">2</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.852em, 1000em, 1.245em, -0.487em); top: -1.302em; left: 0em;"><span style="border-left: 0.499em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 1.25px; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.082em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-577" class="mo">×</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-578" class="mn">0.80</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.278em;" id="MathJax-Span-579" class="mo">=</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.278em;" id="MathJax-Span-580" class="mn">0.80</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.219em;"></span></span></span><span style="border-left: 0em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 1.853em; vertical-align: -0.597em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script id="MathJax-Element-117" type="math/tex">\frac{1}{2}(1-\frac{10}{50}) + \frac{1}{2}(1-\frac{10}{50}) = \frac{1}{2} \times 0.80 + \frac{1}{2} \times 0.80 = 0.80</script></td>
<td><span class="course-quiz-answer-correct" title="Correct" alt="Correct"><span class="icon-ok" alt="Correct"><span class="accessible-text-for-reader">Correct</span></span></span></td>
<td>0.50</td>
<td>This is indeed the correct answer. First of all the Petri net correctly records the remaining and missing tokens after replay, including the 10 tokens produced in the initial place and consumed from the final place.<br> Furthermore, the correct formula is used (the full formula is shown in the explanation of the next question).</td>
</tr>

<td>Total</td>
<td></td>

Which results in c=9, p=9, m=0 and r=0 for <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-125-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-616" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 18px; height: 0px; font-size: 132%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.571em, 1000em, 2.492em, -0.456em); top: -2.165em; left: 0em;"><span id="MathJax-Span-617" class="mrow"><span id="MathJax-Span-618" class="msubsup"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.994em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.625em, 1000em, 2.392em, -0.456em); top: -2.219em; left: 0em;"><span style="font-family: MathJax_Math; font-style: italic;" id="MathJax-Span-619" class="mi">σ<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.001em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.219em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -2.015em; left: 0.54em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-620" class="mn">3</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="border-left: 0em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 0.93em; vertical-align: -0.29em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script id="MathJax-Element-125" type="math/tex">\sigma_3</script> <br><br>

The token-based conformance is calculated by filling in the following formula:<br>
<span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-126-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-621" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; font-style: italic;" id="MathJax-Span-625" class="mi">L</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-626" class="mo">,</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Math; font-style: italic; padding-left: 0.167em;" id="MathJax-Span-627" class="mi">N<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.085em;"></span></span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-628" class="mo">)</span><span style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.278em;" id="MathJax-Span-629" class="mo">=</span><span style="padding-left: 0.398em; padding-right: 0.12em;" id="MathJax-Span-630" class="mfrac"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.499em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.327em, -0.428em); top: -2.576em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.189em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;" id="MathJax-Span-631" class="mn">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.531em, 1000em, 2.327em, -0.452em); top: -1.782em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.189em;"><span style="font-size: 70.7%; </div><div class="course-quiz-question-body">

<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-explanation">
<b>Question Explanation<br><br></b>Alignments based conformance is explained in more detail in lecture 4.7: 'Aligning observed and modeled behavior'.</div>
</div><div class="course-quiz-question-body">
<h3 class="course-quiz-question-number">Question 8</h3>
<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-text">Given the process model below and the following event log: [ &lt; a,b,c,h,i &gt;<span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-131-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-837" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; <br><br><a target="https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/procmin/images/Quizzes/Quiz4-Q4%20model.png"><img src="https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/procmin/images/Quizzes/Quiz4-Q4%20model.png" alt="Quiz4-Q4%20model.png"></a>
<br>
What is the correct alignment-based conformance for this event log, assuming all costs for move on model and move on log, for all activities, are 1?<br>
Hint: first calculate the fitness per trace, as is explained in the lecture. Then calculate the weighted average (or <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Weighted_arithmetic_mean" target="_blank">weighted arithmetic mean</a>) using the trace frequency as weight.</div>

<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-explanation">
<b>Question Explanation<br><br></b>For all traces we can use the trace length plus the shortest path through the model ( &lt; a,b,c,i &gt; ) to normalize the deviation cost.<br>
The trace &lt; a,b,c,h,i &gt; can be aligned with a cost of 1 (a 'move on log' for event 'h'). Hence, <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-133-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-847" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; padding-left: 0.222em;" id="MathJax-Span-854" class="mo">−</span><span style="padding-left: 0.342em; padding-right: 0.12em;" id="MathJax-Span-855" class="mfrac"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; top: -1.302em; left: 0em;"><span style="border-left: 1.419em solid; display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 1.25px; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; The trace &lt; a,b,e,f,g,h,i &gt; can be aligned with a cost of 2 (a 'move on log' for event b and a 'move on model' for activity d). Hence <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-134-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-865" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; The overall fitness of the event log on the given model therefore is <span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span style="" aria-readonly="true" role="textbox" id="MathJax-Element-136-Frame" class="MathJax"><nobr><span id="MathJax-Span-899" class="math"><span style="display: inline-block; <br><br>
Alignments based conformance is explained in more detail in lecture 4.7: 'Aligning observed and modeled behavior'.</div>

<h3 class="course-quiz-question-number">Question 9</h3>
<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-text">Which of the following conformance checking techniques suffers from the problem that the frequency of occurrence of the traces is not considered?</div>

<input dir="auto" class="course-quiz-input" name="answer[62cee8f9aa516b4b71ff5dba69ac1ba6][]" id="gensym_548af590b2422" value="4f467ea4466d0e021ed593e2a651a158" checked="" disabled="" type="radio">Conformance checking using alignments.</td>
<td><span class="course-quiz-answer-incorrect" title="Incorrect" alt="Incorrect"><span class="icon-remove" alt="Incorrect"><span class="accessible-text-for-reader">Inorrect</span></span></span></td>
<td>0.00</td>
<td>Currently conformance checking with alignments is the most robust conformance technique, mainly because it finds an optimal explanation of observed deviations. It also considers the frequency of the traces.<br>
This technique is discussed in more detail in lecture 4.7: 'Aligning observed and modelled behavior'.</td>

<div dir="auto" class="course-quiz-question-explanation">
<b>Question Explanation<br><br></b>Footprint-based conformance is explained in detail in lecture 4.4: 'Conformance checking using causal footprints'.<br>
Conformance checking using token-based replay is explained in more detail in lecture 4.5: 'Conformance checking using token-based replay'.<br>
Alignments based conformance is explained in more detail in lecture 4.7: 'Aligning observed and modeled behavior'.<br>
At the end of each lecture the advantages and disadvantages of each approach are discussed.</div>
